In the opinion of Orrick, Herrington & Sutcliffe LLP, Bond Counsel to the City and County of Honolulu, Hawaii, based upon an analysis of existing laws, regulations, 
rulings and court decisions and assuming, among other matters, the accuracy of certain representations and compliance with certain covenants, and subject to the satisfaction of 
certain conditions and to the occurrence of certain events described hereunder under the heading “FORWARD DELIVERY OF THE SEN IOR SERIES 2025 BONDS AND THE 
JUNIOR SERIES 2025 BONDS” for the Senior Series 2025 Bonds and the Junior Series 2025 Bonds, interest on the Series 2024/2025 Bonds (defined below) is excluded from 
gross income for federal income tax purposes under Section 103 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 (the “Code”).  In the further opinion of Bond Counsel, interest on the Series 
2024/2025 Bonds is not a specific preference item for purposes of the federal individual alternative minimum tax.  Bond Counsel observes that interest on the Series 2024/2025 
Bonds included in adjusted financial statement income of certain corporations is not excluded from the federal corporate alternative minimum tax. Bond Counsel is of the opinion 
that the Series 2024/2025 Bonds and the income therefrom are exempt from all taxation by the State of Hawaii or any county or  other political subdivision thereof,  except 
inheritance, transfer, estate and certain franchise taxes.  Bond Counsel expresses no opinion regarding any other tax consequences related to the ownership or disposition of, or 
the amount, accrual or receipt of interest on, the Series 2024/2025 Bonds.  See “TAX MATTERS” in this Official Statement.

The City and County of Honolulu W astewater System Revenue Bonds (First Bond Resolution) Senior Series 2024A (Green Bonds) (the “Senior Series 2024A Bonds”), 
Senior Series 2024B (Refunding) (the “Senior Series 2024B Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024A Bonds, the “Senior Series 2024 Bonds”) and Senior Series 2025A 
(Forward Refunding) (the “Senior Series 2025 Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024 Bonds, the “Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds”) and the City and County of Honolulu 
Wastewater System Revenue Bonds (Second Bond Resolution) Junior Series 2024A Bonds (Refunding) (the “Junior Series 2024 Bonds”) and Junior Series 2025A (Forward 
Refunding) (the “Junior Series 2025 Bonds” and, together with the Junior Series 2024 Bonds, the “Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024/2025 
Bonds, the “Series 2024/2025 Bonds”) are issuable in fully registered form and when issued will be registered initially in the name of Cede & Co., as nominee of T he Depository 
Trust Company (“DTC”), New York, New York.  So long as DTC or its nominee is the registered owner of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds, purchases of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds 
will be made in book -entry form only, through brokers and dealers who are, or who act through, DTC participants.  Beneficial owners of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds will not 
receive physical delivery of Series 2024/2025 Bond certificates; payment of the principal of and interest and any premium on the Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be made directly to 
DTC or its nominee; and disbursement of such payments to DTC participants will be the responsibility of DTC and disbursement of such payments to the beneficial owners will 
be the responsibility of DTC participants.  Purchases of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds may be made in the denomination of $5,000 or any integral multiple thereof.  
The Senior Series 2024 Bonds and the Junior Series 2024 Bonds bear interest payable on January 1 and July 1 of each year, commencing July 1, 2025. The Senior Series 
2025 Bonds and the Junior Series 2025 Bonds bear interest payable on January 1 and July 1 of each year, commencing January 1,  2026. The Series 2024/2025 Bonds are subject 
to redemption prior to the stated maturity thereof as described herein. Proceeds of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be used to: (i) fund the cost of certain additions and improvements 
to the wastewater system owned by the City and County of Honolulu (the “City and County”), (ii) refund certain outstanding bonds previously issued by the City and County 
pursuant to the First Bond Resolution (as defined below) and the Second Bond Resolution (as defined below), and (iii) pay the costs of issuance of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds.  
The Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be issued by the City and County under a bond resolution, as supplemented (the “First Bond Resolution”), pursuant to which the 
City and County has previously issued bonds and may issue additional bonds on a parity with the Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds, as described herein.  The Senior Series 2024/2025 
Bonds are limited special obligations of the City and County payable solely from, and secured solely by a pledge of, the Net Revenues, proceeds of Bonds held or set asid e under 
the First Bond Resolution, and certain funds and accounts established by the First Bond Resolution, on a parity with all other Bonds issued under the First Bond Resolution.  Such 
pledge of the Net Revenues is senior and superior to any pledge of Net Revenues to secure obligations issued under  any other bond resolution, including the Second Bond 
Resolution. 
The Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be issued by the City and County under a bond resolution, as supplemented (the “Second Bond Resolution”), pursuant to which 
the City and County has previously issued bonds and may issue additional bonds on a parity with the Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds , as described herein.  The Junior Series 
2024/2025 Bonds are limited special obligations of the City and County payable solely from, and secured solely by a pledge of, the Net Revenu es, proceeds of Bonds held or set 
aside under the Second Bond Resolution, and certain funds and accounts established by the Second Bond Resolution, on a parity with all other Bonds issued under the Second 
Bond Resolution.  Such pledge of the Net Revenues is junior in priority and subordinate to any pledge of Net Revenues to secure obligations issued under the First Bond Resolution.   
The Series 2024/2025 Bonds are not a general or moral obligation of the State of Hawaii or any political subdivision thereof, including the City and County, and 
the faith and credit of the State of Hawaii or any political subdivision thereof, including the City and County, are not pledged to the payment of the principal of, premium, 
if any, or interest on the Series 2024/2025 Bonds, and no holder of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds shall have the right to compel the exercise of the taxing power of the State 
of Hawaii or any political subdivision thereof, including the City and County, in connection with any default with respect to the Series 2024/2025 Bonds. 
This cover page contains certain information for quick reference only.  It is not a summary of the bond issue.  Prospective investors must read the entire Official Statement 
(including the Appendices) to obtain information essential to the making of an informed investment decision. Prospective purchasers of the Senior Series 2025 Bonds and the Junior 
Series 2025 Bonds should carefully review the information under the caption “FORWARD DELIVERY OF THE SENIOR SERIES 2025 BONDS AND THE JUNIOR SERIES 2025 
BONDS” before making an investment decision with respect to the Senior Series 2025 Bonds and the Junior Series 2025 Bonds. 
The Series 2024/2025 Bonds  are offered when, as and if issued and received by the Underwriter s, and are subject to the approval of legality by Orrick, Herrington & 
Sutcliffe LLP, Bond Counsel to the City and County. Certain legal matters will be passed upon for the Underwriters by their co-counsel, Dentons US LLP, Honolulu, Hawaii, and 
Katten Muchin Rosenman LLP, New York, New York.  It is expected that the Senior Series 2024 Bonds and the Junior Series 2024 Bonds in definitive form will be available for 
delivery to DTC, in New York, New York, on or about September 25, 2024 and that the Senior Series 2025 Bonds and the Junior Series 2025 Bonds in definitive form will be 
available for delivery to DTC, in New York, New York, on or about April 2, 2025.

INTRODUCTORY STATEMENT 
This Official Statement, which includes the cover page, the inside cover page s and the appendices, provides 
certain information in connection with the issuance by the City and County of Honolulu (the “City and County”) in the State of 
Hawaii (the “State” or “Hawaii”) of $501,070,000 aggregate principal amount of Wastewater System Revenue Bonds ( First 
Bond Resolution) Senior Series 2024A (Green Bonds) (the “Senior Series 2024A Bonds”), Senior Series 2024B (Refunding) (the 
“Senior Series 2024B Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024A Bonds, the “Senior Series 2024 Bonds”) and  Senior 
Series 2025A (Forward Refunding) (the “Senior Series 2025 Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024 Bonds, the 
“Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds”) and the $124,485,000
 aggregate principal amount of Wastewater System Revenue Bonds 
(Second Bond Resolution) Junior Series 2024A Bonds (Refunding) (the “Junior Series 2024 Bonds”) and Junior Series 2025A 
(Forward Refunding) (the “Junior Series 2025 Bonds” and, together with the Junior Series 2024 Bonds, the “Junior Series 
2024/2025 Bonds” and, together with the Senior Series 2024/2024 Bonds, the “Series 2024/2025 Bonds”). 
The Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are to be issued under  and secured by the First Wastewater Revenue Bond 
Resolution adopted by the City Council of the City and County on November 10, 1998 (as amended and supplemented from time 
to time, the “First Bond Resolution”), and the Senior Series 2024/2025 Resolution adopted by the City Council of the City and 
County on August 7, 2024 (the “Senior Series 2024/2025 Resolution”). The Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are also to be issued 
under a certain Bond Series Certificate of the City and County dated the date of this Official Statement, relating to the Senior 
Series 2024/2025 Bonds (the “Senior Series 2024/2025 Certificate”). 
The Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are to be issued under and secured by the Second Wastewater Revenue 
Bond Resolution adopted by the City Council of the City and County on November 10, 1998 (as amended and supplemented 
from time to time, the “Second Bond Resolution”), and the Junior Series 2024/2025 Resolution adopted by the City Council of 
the City and County on August 7, 2024 (the “ Junior Series 2024/2025 Resolution,” and, together with the Senior Series 
2024/2025 Resolution, the “Series 2024/2025 Resolutions”).  The Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are also to be issued under a 
certain Bond Series Certificate of the City and County dated the date of this Official Statement, relating to the Junior Series 
2024/2025 Bonds (the “ Junior Series 2024/2025 Certificate,” and, together with the Senior Series 2024/2025  Certificate, the 
“Series 2024/2024 Certificates”).  The First Bond Resolution and the Second Bond Resolution are each individually referred to 
as a “Bond Resolution” and collectively referred to as the “Bond Resolutions.” 
The capitalization of any word below not conventionally capitalized indicates that such word is defined in the 
First Bond Resolution, the Second Bond Resolution, the Senior Series 2024/2025 Certificate, the Junior Series 2024/2025  
Certificate or this Official Statement.  A glossary of certain terms used in this Official Statement and the First Bond Resolution 
and the Second Bond Resolution is set forth in Appendix B under “Summary of Certain Provisions of the Bond Resolutions – 
Certain Definitions.” 
  
2 
 
Proceeds of the Senior Series 2024A Bonds will be used to: (i) fund the cost of certain additions and 
improvements to the wastewater system owned by the City and County pursuant to the  First Bond Resolution and (ii) pay the 
costs of issuance of such  Senior Series 2024A Bonds. Proceeds of the Senior Series 2024 B Bonds will be used to: (i) advance 
refund certain outstanding bonds previously issued by the City and County pursuant to the First Bond Resolution and (i i) pay the 
costs of issuance of such Senior Series 2024B Bonds.  Proceeds of the Senior Series 20 25 Bonds will be used to: (i) forward  
refund certain outstanding bonds previously issued by the City and County pursuant to the First Bond Resolution and (ii) pay the 
costs of issuance of such Senior Series 2025 Bonds. 
Proceeds of the Junior Series 2024 Bonds will be used to: (i) advance refund certain outstanding bonds 
previously issued by the City and County pursuant to the Second Bond Resolution and (ii) pay the costs of issuance of such 
Junior Series 2024 Bonds.  Proceeds of the Junior Series 2025 Bonds will be used to: (i) forward refund certain outstanding 
bonds previously issued by the City and County pursuant to the Second Bond Resolution and (ii) pay the costs of issuance of 
such Junior Series 2025 Bonds.  See “ESTIMATED SOURCES AND USES OF PROCEEDS” below. 
The Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are the 34
th, 35th and 36th series of bonds (each a “Series” and collectively 
the “Senior Bonds”) issued under and pursuant to the First Bond Resolution and will be secured by and entitled to the protect ion 
of the First Bond Resolution on a parity with all Senior Bonds heretofore issued and to be hereafter issued under and pursuant to 
the First Bond Resolution.  The Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are limited special obligations of the City and County payable 
solely from, and secured solely by a pledge of, the Net Revenues, proceeds of Senior Series 2024/2025 Bonds held or set aside 
under the First Bond Resolution, and certain funds and accounts established by the First Bond Resolution.  Such pledge of the  
Net Revenues is senior and superior to any pledge of the Net Revenues to secure obligations issued under any other bond 
resolution, including the Second Bond Resolution.   
The Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are the 1 3
th and 14th series of bonds (each a “Series” and collectively the 
“Junior Bonds”) issued under and pursuant to the Second Bond Resolution and will be secured by and entitled to the protection  
of the Second Bond Resolution on a parity with all Junior Bonds heretofore issued and to be hereafter issued under and pursua nt 
to the Second Bond Resolution.  The Senior Bonds and the Junior Bonds are collectively referred to as the “Bonds.”  The Junior 
Series 2024/2025 Bonds are limited special obligations of the City and County payable solely from, and secured solely by a 
pledge of, the Net Revenues, proceeds of Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds held or set aside under the Second Bond Resolution, 
and certain funds and accounts established by the Second Bond Resolution.  Such pledge of the Net Revenues is junior in priority 
to the pledge of the Net Revenues to secure obligations issued under the First Bond Resolution, but senior in priority to the  
pledge of the Net Revenues to secure the Department’s outstanding State Revolving Fund loans and any reimbursable general 
obligation bonds issued by the City and County for the benefit of the Department.  See “SECURITY FOR THE BONDS.” 
As of June 30 , 2024, the City and County had $ 2,168,275,000 principal amount of Senior Bonds outstanding.  
As of such date, the City and County also had $ 201,060,000 principal amount of Junior Bonds  outstanding.  The Junior Bonds, 
together with the Department’s outstanding State Revolving Fund loans, are considered to be “ Subordinate Obligations ” for 
purposes of the Bond Resolutions .  All outstanding Senior Bonds and Subordinate Obligations are fixed rate obligations.  See 
“DEBT AND FINANCIAL POLICIES AND INDEBTEDNESS – Indebtedness” herein. 
The Department of Environmental Services (the “Department”) was created on July 1, 1998, as part of a city -
wide reorganization.  The Department has the full and complete authority to manage, control and operate the Wastewater System  
owned or managed and under the jurisdiction of the City and County, including all materials, supplies, equipment and properti es 
used or useful in connection with the Wastewater System.  Previously, the Department of Wastewater Management, created by a 
City Charter change effective July 1, 1993, provided operation, maintenance, planning, design and construction of wastewater 
facilities in the City and County.  The City Charter and Chapter 49, Hawaii Revised Statutes (the “Act”) empower the City and 
County to issue revenue bonds in its name for the purposes of the Wastewater System.  See “ THE CITY AND COUNTY AND 
THE DEPARTMENT.” 
As of June 30, 202 4, the Wastewater System serviced approximately 149,000 separate accounts and a 
population of approximately 780,000, which is approximately 78% of the total resident population of the City and County based 
on the 2023 data book.  The service area covers nearly 600 square miles.  The customer base includes the residential population, 
business and industrial users, and other users located in the service area.  Of the approximately 149,000 accounts, approxima tely 
141,000 are residential, which generate approximately 95% of the total revenue from sewer service charges, and the remaining 
approximately 8,000 accounts are non -residential, which generate approximately 5% of the total revenue from sewer service 
charges.  In the Fiscal Year ended June 30, 2024, the average total volume of wastewater processed by the Wastewater System  
3 
 
was approximately 100.18 million gallons per day (“MGD”), an increase of 4% from Fiscal Year 202 3.  See “THE 
WASTEWATER SYSTEM.” 
The Department is currently undertaking a capital improvement program adopted by the Department and 
approved by the City Council (the “2024- 2028 Capital Improvement Program”).  The 2024- 2028 Capital Improvement Program 
is projected to cost approximately $4.5  billion (in inflated dollars, i.e., adjusted from 202 4 dollars) and is being undertaken for 
the purposes, among others, of meeting the requirements of certain consent decrees, permits, or administrative orders entered  
into by the Department with Federal and State regulatory bodies and reliably serving projected growth in the number of 
customers served by the Wastewater System.  The 2024 -2028 Capital Improvement Program is part of the Department’s 2016-
2035 twenty- year capital improvement program (the “2016- 2035 Capital Improvement Program”).  The 2016- 2035 Capital 
Improvement Program is projected to cost approximately $ 12.3 billion (in inflated dollars) and has been undertaken for the same 
basic purposes as the 2024- 2028 Capital Improvement Program.  The cost of the 2016- 2035 Capital Improvement Program, 
including the 2024-2028 Capital Improvement Program, is expected to be financed primarily from: (i) proceeds of Senior Bonds 
and Subordinate Obligations (including Clean Water State Revolving Fund loans) previously issued and currently available, (ii ) 
proceeds of additional Senior or Junior Bonds (including the Senior Series 2024A Bonds) and Subordinate Obligations (currently 
expected to consist primarily of Clean Water State Revolving Fund loans) to be issued in the future, (iii) Net Revenues of th e 
Wastewater System, and (iv) Wastewater System Facilities Charges.  See “CAPITAL IMPROVEMENT PROGRAM.” 
Pursuant to the Act and the City Charter, the City Council has the power to impose, prescribe and collect rates, 
rentals, fees or charges for the use and services of, and the facilities furnished by, the Wastewater System so that the Wast ewater 
System will be and remain self -sustaining.  The rates, rentals, fees or charges imposed and prescribed are required to produce 
revenues which will be at least sufficient to pay debt service on all revenue bonds issued for the purposes of the Wastewater  
System, including the Senior Bonds and the Subordinate Obligations , including Junior Bonds, to provide reserves therefor, to 
pay the costs of operation, maintenance and repair of the Wastewater System, and to carry out the covenants of all resolutions 
authorizing the issuance of revenue bonds for the purposes of the Wastewater System, including the First Bond Resolution and 
the Second Bond Resolution.  The rates and charges fixed and imposed by the City Council are not subject to approval by any 
federal or state regulatory bodies.  See discussion under “HISTORICAL AND PROJECTED REVENUES, EXPENSES AND 
COVERAGES.”

THE SERIES 2024/2025 BONDS 
General 
The Senior Series 2024/2025  Bonds and the Junior Series 2024/2025 Bonds are secured by and issued 
pursuant to separate resolutions, issuance certificates and other proceedings.  The summary set forth below is presented in a  
consolidated manner for convenience. 
The Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be dated as of the date of their issuance and will bear interest at the rates and 
mature on the dates and in the principal amounts set forth on the inside cover page s of this Official Statement.  The Series 
2024/2025 Bonds will be issued in minimum denominations of $5,000 principal amount.  Interest will accrue on the Senior 
Series 2024 Bonds and the Junior Series 2024 Bonds from the date of their issuance and will be due and payable semiannually on 
January 1 and July 1 of each year, commencing July 1, 2025. Interest will accrue on the Senior Series 2025 Bonds and the Junior 
Series 2025 Bonds from the date of their issuance and will be due and payable semiannually on January 1 and July 1 of each 
year, commencing January 1, 2026. U.S. Bank Trust Company, National Association (successor in interest to U.S. Bank National 
Association) will serve as the initial Paying Agent for the Series 2024/2025 Bonds. 
The Series 2024/2025 Bonds, when issued, will be registered in the name of Cede & Co., as nominee of The 
Depository Trust Company (“DTC”), New York, New York, which will act as securities depository for the Series 2024/2025 
Bonds (together with its successors, if any, in such capacity, the “Securities Depository”).  So long as the Securities Depository 
or its nominee is the registered owner of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds, individual purchases of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds will 
be made in book- entry form only (the “Book- Entry System”), in authorized denominations of $5,000 or integral multiples 
thereof.  Purchasers will not receive certificates representing their interest in the Series 2024/2025 Bonds.  Principal of and 
interest on the Series 2024/2025 Bonds will be paid to the Securities Depository, which will in turn remit such principal and 
interest to its Direct Participants (as defined in Appendix C , “Book-Entry Only System”), for subsequent distribution to Indirect 
Participants (as defined in Appendix C , “Book-Entry Only System”) and Beneficial Owners (as defined in Appendix C , “Book-
Entry Only System ”) of the Series 2024/2025 Bonds.  The Series 2024/2025 Bonds may be transferred or exchanged in the 
manner described in the Series 2024/2025 Bonds and as referenced in accompanying proceedings of the City and County.  See 
Appendix C, “Book- Entry System” for certain information regarding the Book- Entry System maintained by DTC, as Security 
Depository. 
Green Bonds Designation 
The Department is self -designating the Senior Series 2024A Bonds as “Green Bonds” based on the intended 
use of proceeds of the Senior Series 2024A Bonds to finance the costs of certain additions and improvements to the Wastewater 
System. The Department’s Green Bonds designation reflects the use of the proceeds of the Senior Series 2024A Bonds in a 
manner that is consistent with the Green Bond Principles, as promulgated by the International Capital Market Association.  
 Process for Evaluation and Selection 
  The Department maintains and updates at least annually a long -range Capital Improvement Program (the 
“CIP”). The Department’s long-range CIP process, design standards, permitting and 2010 Consent Decree requirements guide 
the process for project evaluation and selection as does the Department’s objective of providing safe and reliable facilities to 
process the wastewater discharge of all sewer customers throughout Oahu.  The classes of CIP projects include system 
expansion, system upgrade, and replacement/rehabilitation. See “CAPITAL IMPROVEMENT PROGRAM” below for 
additional information regarding the CIP and capital expenditures and projects for the Wastewater System . 
  
8 
 
 Management of Proceeds 
  Proceeds from the Senior Series 2024A Bonds will be used to finance the costs of certain additions and 
improvements to the Wastewater System. Net of certain transaction costs, the proceeds of the Senior Series 2024A Bonds will be 
tracked and deposited into one or more separate accounts and will be used to finance eligible projects. 
 Reporting 
  The Department intends to produce annual update reports on the impact of the Senior Series 2024A Bonds on 
various green projects until the proceeds have been fully allocated. 
 Not Suitable Investment for all Investors Seeking Exposure to Green Assets 
  The purpose of designating the Senior Series 2024A Bonds as “Green Bonds” is to allow the owners of the 
Senior Series 2024A Bonds to invest directly in bonds which finance environmentally beneficial projects. There is currently no 
clearly-defined definition (legal, regulatory or otherwise) of, nor market consensus as to what constitutes, a “green,” 
“environmental,” “sustainable” or equivalently -labeled project, or as to what precise attributes are required for a particular 
project to be defined as “green,” “environmental,” “sustainable” or such other equivalent label, and nor can any assurance be  
given that such a clear definition or consensus will develop over time. Accordingly, although the Department anticipates that  
financed projects will be aligned with the Green Bond Principles, no assurance can be given to investors that the financed 
projects will meet any or all investor expectations regarding such “green,” “environmental,” “sustainable” or other equivalently -
labeled performance objectives, or that any adverse environmental, sustainable and/or other impacts will not occur during the  
operation and maintenance of such projects. 
  The term “Green Bonds” is neither defined in nor related to provisions in the First Bond Resolution. The term 
“Green Bonds” is solely for identification purpose and is not intended to provide or imply that the owners of the Senior Series 
2024A Bonds are entitled to any security other than that described under the heading “SECURITY FOR THE BONDS” below.
